\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{_s32_k148__features_8h_abbb60c04a7dfc39b282785ddd6e7b60b}{NO\+\_\+\+PERIPHERAL\+\_\+\+FEATURE}}~(0U)         /$\ast$ It\textquotesingle{}s not a peripheral instance, there is no peripheral feature. $\ast$/
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Peripheral instance features List of features that are supported by a peripheral instance. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{_s32_k148__features_8h_a6c1f0cfa24bb9ee64bb4a4f9c55c06cf}{HAS\+\_\+\+CLOCK\+\_\+\+GATING\+\_\+\+IN\+\_\+\+SIM}}~(1U $<$$<$ 0U)   /$\ast$ Clock gating is implemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___s_i_m___peripheral___access___layer_ga3dd2f4c4bfb41778902b4b5350143d9e}{SIM}} (it\textquotesingle{}s not in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___p_c_c___peripheral___access___layer_ga2723ba3b5ec6ca3bf76a1068bebdc624}{PCC}}) $\ast$/
\item 
\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{_s32_k148__features_8h_a19687eab957bec590aeba95d48756562}{HAS\+\_\+\+MULTIPLIER}}~(1U $<$$<$ 1U)   /$\ast$ Multiplier is implemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___p_c_c___peripheral___access___layer_ga2723ba3b5ec6ca3bf76a1068bebdc624}{PCC}} $\ast$/
\item 
\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{_s32_k148__features_8h_a9e12a0ff956e597bf5634e43e0db27dc}{HAS\+\_\+\+DIVIDER}}~(1U $<$$<$ 2U)   /$\ast$ Divider is implemented in \mbox{\hyperlink{group___p_c_c___peripheral___access___layer_ga2723ba3b5ec6ca3bf76a1068bebdc624}{PCC}} $\ast$/
\item 
\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{_s32_k148__features_8h_aea468e1e6eeb0250b74fd43fd0dc0540}{HAS\+\_\+\+PROTOCOL\+\_\+\+CLOCK\+\_\+\+FROM\+\_\+\+ASYNC1}}~(1U $<$$<$ 3U)   /$\ast$ Functional clock source is provided by the first asynchronous clock. $\ast$/
\item

\item 
\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{_s32_k148__features_8h_a209dcc06f56755ee98dfd26d6938a68e}{HAS\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+CLOCK\+\_\+\+FROM\+\_\+\+BUS\+\_\+\+CLOCK}}~(1U $<$$<$ 5U)   /$\ast$ Interface clock is provided by the bus clock. $\ast$/
\item 
\#define \mbox{\hyperlink{_s32_k148__features_8h_a676dd3d3a75c086e09a91b2b197f0607}{HAS\+\_\+\+INT\+\_\+\+CLOCK\+\_\+\+FROM\+\_\+\+SYS\+\_\+\+CLOCK}}~(1U $<$$<$ 6U)   /$\ast$ Interface clock is provided by the sys clock. $\ast$/
\item

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{dma\_request\_source\_t}{dma\_request\_source\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{_s32_k148__features_8h_ad052948ef0b5730afc6ce6101c34ae47}{dma\+\_\+request\+\_\+source\+\_\+t}}}



Structure for the DMA hardware request. 

Defines the structure for the DMA hardware request collections. The user can configure the hardware request into DMAMUX to trigger the DMA transfer accordingly. The index of the hardware request varies according to the to SoC. \begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
